\"\"\"\n   103→    Function/method decorator to deprecate some or all positional arguments.\n   104→\n   105→    The decorated function will map any positional arguments after the ``*`` to\n   106→    the corresponding keyword arguments and issue a deprecation warning.\n   107→\n   108→    The decorator takes two arguments: a RemovedInDjangoXXWarning warning\n   109→    category and a list of parameter names that have been changed from\n   110→    positional-or-keyword to keyword-only, in their original positional order.\n   111→\n   112→    Works on both functions and methods. To apply to a class constructor,\n   113→    decorate its __init__() method. To apply to a staticmethod or classmethod,\n   114→    use @deprecate_posargs after @staticmethod or @classmethod.\n   115→\n   116→    Example: to deprecate passing option1 or option2 as posargs, change::\n   117→\n   118→        def some_func(request, option1, option2=True):\n   119→            ...\n   120→\n   121→    to::\n   122→\n   123→        @deprecate_posargs(RemovedInDjangoXXWarning, [\"option1\", \"option2\"])\n   124→        def some_func(request, *, option1, option2=True):\n   125→            ...\n   126→\n   127→    After the deprecation period, remove the decorator (but keep the ``*``)::\n   128→\n   129→        def some_func(request, *, option1, option2=True):\n   130→            ...\n   131→\n   132→    Caution: during the deprecation period, do not add any new *positional*\n   133→    parameters or change the remaining ones. For example, this attempt to add a\n   134→    new param would break code using the deprecated posargs::\n   135→\n   136→        @deprecate_posargs(RemovedInDjangoXXWarning, [\"option1\", \"option2\"])\n   137→        def some_func(request, wrong_new_param=None, *, option1, option2=True):\n   138→            # Broken: existing code may pass a value intended as option1 in the\n   139→            # wrong_new_param position.\n   140→            ...\n   141→\n   142→    However, it's acceptable to add new *keyword-only* parameters and to\n   143→    re-order the existing ones, so long as the list passed to\n   144→    @deprecate_posargs is kept in the original posargs order. This change will\n   145→    work without breaking existing code::\n   146→\n   147→        @deprecate_posargs(RemovedInDjangoXXWarning, [\"option1\", \"option2\"])\n   148→        def some_func(request, *, new_param=None, option2=True, option1):\n   149→            ...\n   150→\n   151→    The @deprecate_posargs decorator adds a small amount of overhead. In most\n   152→    cases it won't be significant, but use with care in performance-critical\n   153→    code paths.\n   154→    \"\"\"\n   155→\n   156→    def decorator(func):\n   157→        if isinstance(func, type):\n   158→            raise TypeError(\n   159→                \"@deprecate_posargs cannot be applied to a class. (Apply it \"\n   160→                \"to the __init__ method.)\"\n   161→            )\n   162→        if isinstance(func, classmethod):\n   163→            raise TypeError(\"Apply @classmethod before @deprecate_posargs.\")\n   164→        if isinstance(func, staticmethod):\n   165→            raise TypeError(\"Apply @staticmethod before @deprecate_posargs.\")\n   166→\n   167→        params = signature(func).parameters\n   168→        num_by_kind = Counter(param.kind for param in params.values())\n   169→\n   170→        if num_by_kind[inspect.Parameter.VAR_POSITIONAL] > 0:\n   171→            raise TypeError(\n   172→                \"@deprecate_posargs() cannot be used with variable positional `*args`.\"\n   173→            )\n   174→\n   175→        num_positional_params = (\n   176→            num_by_kind[inspect.Parameter.POSITIONAL_ONLY]\n   177→            + num_by_kind[inspect.Parameter.POSITIONAL_OR_KEYWORD]\n   178→        )\n   179→        num_keyword_only_params = num_by_kind[inspect.Parameter.KEYWORD_ONLY]\n   180→        if num_keyword_only_params < 1:\n   181→            raise TypeError(\n   182→                \"@deprecate_posargs() requires at least one keyword-only parameter \"\n   183→                \"(after a `*` entry in the parameters list).\"\n   184→            )\n   185→        if any(\n   186→            name not in params or params[name].kind != inspect.Parameter.KEYWORD_ONLY\n   187→            for name in remappable_names\n   188→        ):\n   189→            raise TypeError(\n   190→                \"@deprecate_posargs() requires all remappable_names to be \"\n   191→                \"keyword-only parameters.\"\n   192→            )\n   193→\n   194→        num_remappable_args = len(remappable_names)\n   195→        max_positional_args = num_positional_params + num_remappable_args\n   196→\n   197→        func_name = func.__name__\n   198→        if func_name == \"__init__\":\n   199→            # Report duplicate names in the original parameter order.\n   229→                conflicts_str = \", \".join(\n   230→                    f\"'{name}'\" for name in remapped_names if name in conflicts\n   231→                )\n   232→                raise TypeError(\n   233→                    f\"{func_name}() got both deprecated positional and keyword \"\n   234→                    f\"argument values for {conflicts_str}.\"\n   235→                )\n   236→\n   237→            # Do the remapping.\n   238→            remapped_kwargs = dict(\n   239→                zip(remapped_names, args[num_positional_params:], strict=True)\n   240→            )\n   241→            remaining_args = args[:num_positional_params]\n   242→            updated_kwargs = kwargs | remapped_kwargs\n   243→\n   244→            # decorator takes two arguments: a RemovedInDjangoXXWarning warning\n    category and a list of parameter names that have been changed from\n    positional-or-keyword to keyword-only, in their original positional order.\n\n    Works on both functions and methods. To apply to a staticmethod or classmethod,\n    use @deprecate_posargs after @staticmethod or @classmethod.\n\n    Example: to deprecate passing option1 or option2 as posargs, change::\n\n        def some_func(request, option1, option2=True):\n            ...\n\n    to::\n\n        @deprecate_posargs(RemovedInDjangoXXWarning, [\"option1\", \"option2\"])\n        def some_func(request, *, option1, option2=True):\n            ...\n\n    After the deprecation period, remove the decorator (but keep the ``*``)::\n\n        def some_func(request, *, option1, option2=True):\n            ...\n\n    Caution: during the deprecation period, do not add any new *positional*\n    parameters or change the remaining ones. take the first one\n            return x_forwarded_for.split(\",\")[0].strip()\n        return request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"\")\n\n    def _get_cache_key(self, ip):\n        \"\"\"Generate a cache key for the given IP address.\"\"\"\n        return f\"rate_limit:{ip}\"\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the request from the client IP exceeds the rate limit.\n\n        Returns HttpResponseTooManyRequests (429) if limit exceeded,\n        None otherwise to allow the request to proceed.\n        \"\"\"\n        client_ip = self._get_client_ip(request)\n        if not client_ip:\n            # If we can't determine the IP, allow the request\n            return None\n\n        cache_key = self._get_cache_key(client_ip)\n\n        # Get the current request count for this IP\n        request_count = cache.get(cache_key, 0)\n\n        # Check if the limit has been exceeded\n        if request_count >= self.rate_limit_requests:\n            return HttpResponseTooManyRequests()\n\n        # Increment the request count and set the cache with expiry\n        cache.set(cache_key, request_count + 1, self.rate_limit_window)\n\n        # Allow the request to proceed\n        return None\n","numLines":71,"startLine":1,"totalLines":71}}}
